  376 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  377 -- INTERNALS and main scanner engine
  378 
  379 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  380 #  define ILIT(n) n#
  381 #  define IBOX(n) (I# (n))
  382 #  define FAST_INT Int#
  383 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  384 #  if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
  385 #    define GTE(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n >=# m))
  386 #    define EQ(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n ==# m))
  387 #  else
  388 #    define GTE(n,m) (n >=# m)
  389 #    define EQ(n,m) (n ==# m)
  390 #  endif
  391 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n +# m)
  392 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n -# m)
  393 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n *# m)
  394 #  define NEGATE(n) (negateInt# (n))
  395 #  define IF_GHC(x) (x)
  396 #else
  397 #  define ILIT(n) (n)
  398 #  define IBOX(n) (n)
  399 #  define FAST_INT Int
  400 #  define GTE(n,m) (n >= m)
  401 #  define EQ(n,m) (n == m)
  402 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n + m)
  403 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n - m)
  404 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n * m)
  405 #  define NEGATE(n) (negate (n))
  406 #  define IF_GHC(x)
  407 #endif
  408 
  409 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  410 data AlexAddr = AlexA# Addr#
  411 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  412 
  413 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt16OffAddr #-}
  414 alexIndexInt16OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  415 alexIndexInt16OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  416 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  417   narrow16Int# i
  418   where
  419         i    = word2Int# ((high `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` low)
  420         high = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  421         low  = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  422         off' = off *# 2#
  423 #else
  424 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  425   GHC.Exts.int16ToInt#
  426 #endif
  427     (indexInt16OffAddr# arr off)
  428 #endif
  429 #else
  430 alexIndexInt16OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
  431 #endif
  432 
  433 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  434 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt32OffAddr #-}
  435 alexIndexInt32OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  436 alexIndexInt32OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  437 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  438   narrow32Int# i
  439   where
  440    i    = word2Int# ((b3 `uncheckedShiftL#` 24#) `or#`
  441                      (b2 `uncheckedShiftL#` 16#) `or#`
  442                      (b1 `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` b0)
  443    b3   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 3#)))
  444    b2   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 2#)))
  445    b1   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  446    b0   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  447    off' = off *# 4#
  448 #else
  449 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  450   GHC.Exts.int32ToInt#
  451 #endif
  452     (indexInt32OffAddr# arr off)
  453 #endif
  454 #else
  455 alexIndexInt32OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
  456 #endif
  457 
  458 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  459 -- GHC >= 503, unsafeAt is available from Data.Array.Base.
  460 quickIndex = unsafeAt
  461 #else
  462 quickIndex = (Data.Array.!)
  463 #endif
  464 
  465 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  466 -- Main lexing routines
  467 
  468 data AlexReturn a
  469   = AlexEOF
  470   | AlexError  !AlexInput
  471   | AlexSkip   !AlexInput !Int
  472   | AlexToken  !AlexInput !Int a
  473 
  474 -- alexScan :: AlexInput -> StartCode -> AlexReturn a
  475 alexScan input__ IBOX(sc)
  476   = alexScanUser undefined input__ IBOX(sc)
  477 
  478 alexScanUser user__ input__ IBOX(sc)
  479   = case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  480   (AlexNone, input__') ->
  481     case alexGetByte input__ of
  482       Nothing ->
  483 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  484                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("End of input.") $
  485 #endif
  486                                    AlexEOF
  487       Just _ ->
  488 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  489                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("Error.") $
  490 #endif
  491                                    AlexError input__'
  492 
  493   (AlexLastSkip input__'' len, _) ->
  494 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  495     Debug.Trace.trace ("Skipping.") $
  496 #endif
  497     AlexSkip input__'' len
  498 
  499   (AlexLastAcc k input__''' len, _) ->
  500 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  501     Debug.Trace.trace ("Accept.") $
  502 #endif
  503     AlexToken input__''' len ((Data.Array.!) alex_actions k)
  504 
  505 
  506 -- Push the input through the DFA, remembering the most recent accepting
  507 -- state it encountered.
  508 
  509 alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input len input__ s last_acc =
  510   input__ `seq` -- strict in the input
  511   let
  512   new_acc = (check_accs (alex_accept `quickIndex` IBOX(s)))
  513   in
  514   new_acc `seq`
  515   case alexGetByte input__ of
  516      Nothing -> (new_acc, input__)
  517      Just (c, new_input) ->
  518 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  519       Debug.Trace.trace ("State: " ++ show IBOX(s) ++ ", char: " ++ show c ++ " " ++ (show . chr . fromIntegral) c) $
  520 #endif
  521       case fromIntegral c of { IBOX(ord_c) ->
  522         let
  523                 base   = alexIndexInt32OffAddr alex_base s
  524                 offset = PLUS(base,ord_c)
  525 
  526                 new_s = if GTE(offset,ILIT(0))
  527                           && let check  = alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_check offset
  528                              in  EQ(check,ord_c)
  529                           then alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_table offset
  530                           else alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_deflt s
  531         in
  532         case new_s of
  533             ILIT(-1) -> (new_acc, input__)
  534                 -- on an error, we want to keep the input *before* the
  535                 -- character that failed, not after.
  536             _ -> alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input
  537 #ifdef ALEX_LATIN1
  538                    PLUS(len,ILIT(1))
  539                    -- issue 119: in the latin1 encoding, *each* byte is one character
  540 #else
  541                    (if c < 0x80 || c >= 0xC0 then PLUS(len,ILIT(1)) else len)
  542                    -- note that the length is increased ONLY if this is the 1st byte in a char encoding)
  543 #endif
  544                    new_input new_s new_acc
  545       }
  546   where
  547         check_accs (AlexAccNone) = last_acc
  548         check_accs (AlexAcc a  ) = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  549         check_accs (AlexAccSkip) = AlexLastSkip  input__ IBOX(len)
  550 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  551         check_accs (AlexAccPred a predx rest)
  552            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  553            = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  554            | otherwise
  555            = check_accs rest
  556         check_accs (AlexAccSkipPred predx rest)
  557            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  558            = AlexLastSkip input__ IBOX(len)
  559            | otherwise
  560            = check_accs rest
  561 #endif
  562 
  563 data AlexLastAcc
  564   = AlexNone
  565   | AlexLastAcc !Int !AlexInput !Int
  566   | AlexLastSkip     !AlexInput !Int
  567 
  568 data AlexAcc user
  569   = AlexAccNone
  570   | AlexAcc Int
  571   | AlexAccSkip
  572 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  573   | AlexAccPred Int (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  574   | AlexAccSkipPred (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  575 
  576 type AlexAccPred user = user -> AlexInput -> Int -> AlexInput -> Bool
  577 
  578 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  579 -- Predicates on a rule
  580 
  581 alexAndPred p1 p2 user__ in1 len in2
  582   = p1 user__ in1 len in2 && p2 user__ in1 len in2
  583 
  584 --alexPrevCharIsPred :: Char -> AlexAccPred _
  585 alexPrevCharIs c _ input__ _ _ = c == alexInputPrevChar input__
  586 
  587 alexPrevCharMatches f _ input__ _ _ = f (alexInputPrevChar input__)
  588 
  589 --alexPrevCharIsOneOfPred :: Array Char Bool -> AlexAccPred _
  590 alexPrevCharIsOneOf arr _ input__ _ _ = arr Data.Array.! alexInputPrevChar input__
  591 
  592 --alexRightContext :: Int -> AlexAccPred _
  593 alexRightContext IBOX(sc) user__ _ _ input__ =
  594      case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  595           (AlexNone, _) -> False
  596           _ -> True
  597         -- TODO: there's no need to find the longest
  598         -- match when checking the right context, just
  599         -- the first match will do.
  600 #endif
  601 {-# LINE 103 "src/SAWScript/Lexer.x" #-}
  602 -- token helpers
  603 
  604 plain ::                   (Pos -> Text -> Token Pos)   -> Pos -> Text -> Token Pos
  605 xform :: (Text -> Text) -> (Pos -> Text -> Token Pos)   -> Pos -> Text -> Token Pos
  606 addon :: (Text -> a) -> (Pos -> Text -> a -> Token Pos) -> Pos -> Text -> Token Pos
  607 
  608 plain   tok pos txt = tok pos txt         -- ^ just the contents
  609 xform f tok pos txt = tok pos (f txt)     -- ^ transform contents
  610 addon f tok pos txt = tok pos txt (f txt) -- ^ also variant contents
  611 
  612 -- fetch a value via Read
  613 --
  614 -- XXX: we should not use this for string literals, because as much as
  615 -- it's convenient to have the stdlib decode escape sequences for us,
  616 -- the escape sequences available in SAWScript strings should properly
  617 -- be defined by SAWScript (that is, explicitly here) and not by
  618 -- what's in GHC's standard library.
  619 --
  620 -- FUTURE: it would be nice to get the source position into the panic
  621 -- message in case it ever actually happens, but that seems difficult
  622 -- to arrange.
  623 read' :: Read a => Text -> a
  624 read' txt = case readMaybe txt' of
  625     Just x -> x
  626     Nothing -> panic "Lexer" ["Failed to decode string or number literal", txt']
  627   where txt' = Text.unpack txt
  628 
  629 -- drop the {{ }} or {| |} from Cryptol blocks
  630 readCode :: Text -> Text
  631 readCode txt = Text.drop 2 $ Text.dropEnd 2 txt
  632 
  633 -- read a binary integer
  634 readBin :: Text -> Integer
  635 readBin s = case readInt 2 isDigit cvt (Text.unpack s') of
  636               [(a, "")] -> a
  637               _         -> error $ "Cannot read a binary number from: " ++ show s
  638   where cvt c = ord c - ord '0'
  639         isDigit c = c == '0' || c == '1'
  640         s' | "0b" `Text.isPrefixOf` s = Text.drop 2 s
  641            | "0B" `Text.isPrefixOf` s = Text.drop 2 s
  642            | True                     = s
  643 
  644 
  645 -- alex support and lexer mechanism
  646 
  647 -- current position
  648 data AlexPos = AlexPos {
  649     apLine :: !Int,
  650     apCol :: !Int
  651   }
  652 
  653 -- input state
  654 type AlexInput = (
  655     AlexPos,    -- ^ Current position
  656     Text        -- ^ Remaining input
  657   )
  658 
  659 -- initial position
  660 startPos :: AlexPos
  661 startPos = AlexPos { apLine = 1, apCol = 1 }
  662 
  663 -- feed alex a byte describing the current char
  664 -- this came from Cryptol's lexer, which came from LexerUtils, which
  665 -- adapted the technique used in GHC's lexer.
  666 byteForChar :: Char -> Word8
  667 byteForChar c
  668   | c <= '\7' = non_graphic
  669   | Char.isAscii c = fromIntegral (ord c)
  670   | otherwise = case Char.generalCategory c of
  671       Char.LowercaseLetter       -> lower
  672       Char.OtherLetter           -> lower
  673       Char.UppercaseLetter       -> upper
  674       Char.TitlecaseLetter       -> upper
  675       Char.DecimalNumber         -> digit
  676       Char.OtherNumber           -> digit
  677       Char.ConnectorPunctuation  -> symbol
  678       Char.DashPunctuation       -> symbol
  679       Char.OtherPunctuation      -> symbol
  680       Char.MathSymbol            -> symbol
  681       Char.CurrencySymbol        -> symbol
  682       Char.ModifierSymbol        -> symbol
  683       Char.OtherSymbol           -> symbol
  684       Char.Space                 -> sp
  685       Char.ModifierLetter        -> other
  686       Char.NonSpacingMark        -> other
  687       Char.SpacingCombiningMark  -> other
  688       Char.EnclosingMark         -> other
  689       Char.LetterNumber          -> other
  690       Char.OpenPunctuation       -> other
  691       Char.ClosePunctuation      -> other
  692       Char.InitialQuote          -> other
  693       Char.FinalQuote            -> tick
  694       _                          -> non_graphic
  695   where
  696   -- CAUTION: these must match the $uni* values at the top of the file
  697   non_graphic     = 0
  698   upper           = 1
  699   lower           = 2
  700   digit           = 3
  701   symbol          = 4
  702   sp              = 5
  703   other           = 6
  704   tick            = 7
  705 
  706 -- input handler for alex
  707 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Word8, AlexInput)
  708 alexGetByte (pos, text) = fmap doGet $ Text.uncons text
  709     where
  710       doGet (c, text') = (byteForChar c, (move pos c, text'))
  711       move pos c = case c of
  712           '\n' -> AlexPos { apLine = apLine pos + 1, apCol = 1 }
  713           _ -> pos { apCol = apCol pos + 1 }
  714 
  715 -- the lexer we're generating doesn't use this hook
  716 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  717 alexInputPrevChar _ = panic "Lexer" ["alexInputPrevChar"]
  718 
  719 -- read the text of a file, passing in the filename for use in positions
  720 scanTokens :: FilePath -> Text -> [Token Pos]
  721 scanTokens filename str = go (startPos, str)
  722   where
  723     fillPos pos height width =
  724         let startLine = apLine pos
  725             startCol = apCol pos
  726             endLine = startLine + height
  727             endCol = startCol + width
  728         in
  729         Range filename startLine startCol endLine endCol
  730 
  731     go inp@(pos, str) = case alexScan inp 0 of
  732         AlexEOF ->
  733             let pos' = fillPos pos 0 0 in
  734             [TEOF pos' "EOF"]
  735         AlexError (pos, _) ->
  736             let line' = show $ apLine pos
  737                 col' = show $ apCol pos
  738             in
  739             error $ line' ++ ":" ++ col' ++ ": unspecified lexical error"
  740         AlexSkip inp' len ->
  741             go inp'
  742         AlexToken inp' len act ->
  743             let text = Text.take len str
  744                 (height, width) = case reverse $ Text.lines text of
  745                     [] -> (0, 0)
  746                     [line] -> (0, Text.length line)
  747                     last : lines -> (length lines, Text.length last)
  748                 pos' = fillPos pos height width
  749             in
  750             act pos' text : go inp'
  751 
  752 -- postprocess to drop comments (this allows comments to be nested)
  753 dropComments :: [Token Pos] -> [Token Pos]
  754 dropComments = go 0
  755   where go :: Int -> [Token Pos] -> [Token Pos]
  756         go _  []                 = []
  757         go !i (TCmntS _ _ : ts)  = go (i+1) ts
  758         go !i (TCmntE _ _ : ts)
  759          | i > 0                 = go (i-1) ts
  760         go !i (t : ts)
  761          | i /= 0                = go i ts
  762          | True                  = t : go i ts
  763 
  764 -- entry point
  765 lexSAW :: FilePath -> Text -> [Token Pos]
  766 lexSAW f text = dropComments $ scanTokens f text
  767 
  768 -- alternate monadic entry point (XXX: does this have any value?)
  769 scan :: Monad m => FilePath -> Text -> m [Token Pos]
  770 scan f = return . lexSAW f
